0                                      2              *******************************************************************
                                       3              *                                                                 *
                                       4              *     MILTEN/370 - Release VI - Class I - Stanford Proprietary    *
                                       5              *                                                                 *
                                       6              *******************************************************************
                                       7                       HIBAL
                                     995              **
                                     996              **  MILTEN/IV.  MILTEN has been re-written in this version.  Most
                                     997              **    things (sessions, subsystem blocks, etc.) are now dynamically
                                     998              **    built.  The dispatcher is based on queues.  A major change is
                                     999              **    that all command processing is now done by the subsystem.
                                    1000              **    MILTEN provides the necessary information by responding to
                                    1001              **    "control" requests from the subsystem.  The ALCB is provided
                                    1002              **    for compatability only, and is not used by MILTEN.
                                    1003              **
                                    1004              **                                                  9/79, Jim Nisbet
                                    1005              **
                                    1006              **
                                    1007              **  MILTEN/V.  This is the MVS/SP version of MILTEN.  Some things
                                    1008              **    have been cleaned up since MILTEN/IV.  The teleprocessing I/O
                                    1009              **    now uses the STARTIO interface instead of EXCP.  MILTEN's
                                    1010              **    "failsoft" recovery has been extended, dumps now use sysout
                                    1011              **    spinoff to produce the dump when the error occurs.
                                    1012              **    In addition, MVS failure recovery routines (FRRs) allow
                                    1013              **    failsoft recovery to now work for IOS exit routines
                                    1014              **    (appendages).
                                    1015              **
                                    1016              **                                                  4/82, Jim Nisbet
                                    1017              **
                                    1018              **
                                    1019              **  MILTEN/VI.  This is the MVS-XA version of MILTEN.  Not all that
                                    1020              **    much needed to be changed to allow MILTEN to run under MVS-XA.
                                    1021              **    This version will either run under MVS-370 or MVS-XA.
                                    1022              **
                                    1023              **                                                  4/83, Jim Nisbet
                                    1024              **
                                    1025              **  Removed support for all MILTEN front end modules except the ELF.
                                    1026              **
                                    1027              **                                                  10/97, Mike Durket
                                    1028              **
